<A NAME="navavarnams"></A>

<HR>

<center> <b> <font color="red"> Kamalamba Navavarna Krithis </font> </b>   </center>

<HR>

Note: <a href="#srimahaganapathi"> Sri Mahaganapathi (Gowlai) </a> 
and 
<a href="#balasubramanyam"> Balasubramanyam (Surutti) </a> 
are invocation songs for Ganesha and Subramanya respectively, sung before the navavarna krithis.

<A NAME="kamalambike"></A>
